Most of Taoran Road is under construction. Opposite the hotel is a gas station, and on the other side are several catering companies that are very convenient for dining. It is completely within 5 minutes on foot. Although the hotelâ€™s buffet is also very famous, it is still a meal for going out. The breakfast in the hotel is mostly Chinese, with a lot of stir-fried dishes, western style, fruits, and drinks. The waiter in the restaurant is very proactive and cleans up the table meticulously. The room is large in size, especially the bathroom is oversized, separated from wet and dry. The service staff is responsive, and the service is thoughtful and prompt. Parking is very convenient. There are many parking spaces in the underground parking lot, and there are also some parking spaces on the ground. To go out, just scan the QR code and enter the car number at the front desk. Letâ€™s talk about the shortcomings, first: there is a comb left by the previous one for the guests next to the bed in the door room. Second: The curtain opens and closes automatically but there is a gap in the middle, which causes the morning sun to shine directly on my face. The problem is that I can't cover it manually. Third: Such a big room. The double bed is 1.2 meters long and it is very uncomfortable to sleep. It can be changed to 1.5 meters.
